<script>
    var mbNafta = window.mbNafta || {};
    mbNafta.ns = function() {
        var obj = window.mbNafta;
        for (var x = 0, len = arguments.length; x < len; x++) {
            var ns = arguments[x];
            obj[ns] = obj[ns] || {};
            obj = obj[ns];
        }
        return obj;
    };

    var mbDSDataLayer = window.mbDSDataLayer || {};
    mbDSDataLayer.ns = function() {
        var obj = window.mbDSDataLayer;
        for (var x = 0, len = arguments.length; x < len; x++) {
            var ns = arguments[x];
            obj[ns] = obj[ns] || {};
            obj = obj[ns];
        }
        return obj;
    };

    /*
     * Public methods on the mbNafta namespace for loading dependency types.
     * Please see documentation below for each method type
     *
     * @method loadScript
     * Creates an collection of dependencies based on the type and adds
     * the collection to the mbNafta[type] namespace
     * @param type {String} Type of dependency to load
     * @param names {String|Array} Name(s) of dependency to load
     *
     * eg:
     * mbNafta.loadScript('apps', ['main', 'special-offers']);
     * mbNafta.apps => ['main', 'special-offers']
     *
     * As a shortcut, each dependency type has its own method.
     * loadApps([]) | loadExternalLibraries([]) | loadPlugins([])
     * Each of these can independently be used and in any order.
     */

    /**
     * @method mbNafta.loadScript
     * @param type {String} Application type (apps, plugin)
     * @param names {Array} Collection of dependency names
     */
    mbNafta.loadScript = function(type, names) {
        mbNafta[type] = mbNafta[type] || [];

        if(Array.isArray(names)) {
            names.forEach(function(name) {
                if(mbNafta[type].indexOf(name) === -1) {
                    mbNafta[type].push(name);
                }
            });
        } else if (typeof names === 'string' && !mbNafta.apps.includes(names)) {
            mbNafta[type].push(names);
        }
    };

    /**
     * @method mbNafta.loadExternalLibraries
     * @description Adds a list of external library dependency paths to the mbNafta.externalLibraries array
     * @param externalLibrariesPaths {Array} Collection of external library paths
     */
    mbNafta.loadExternalLibraries = function(externalLibrariesPaths) {
        mbNafta.loadScript('externalLibraries', externalLibrariesPaths);
    };

    /**
     * @method mbNafta.loadApps
     * @description Adds a list of app dependency names to the mbNafta.apps array
     * @param appNames {Array} Collection of app names
     */
    mbNafta.loadApps = function(appNames) {
        mbNafta.loadScript('apps', appNames);
    };

    /**
     * @method mbNafta.loadPlugins
     * @description Adds a list of plugin dependency names to the mbNafta.plugins array
     * @param pluginNames {Array} Collection of plugin names
     */
    mbNafta.loadPlugins = function(pluginNames) {
        mbNafta.loadScript('plugins', pluginNames);
    };
</script>

<div class="title-hero">
<section class="title-hero wrapper module-separator" data-analytics-container="{'blade':'title-hero'}">
<h1 class="title-hero__title"> Privacy Statement </h1>
<p class="title-hero__sub-heading"> Learn about the information we collect through the MBUSA platform, how we use that information, and your options for participation. </p>
<p class="title-hero__sub-heading"> Effective: July 1, 2020 </p>
</section>
</div>
<!--*/ Intro */-->
<div class="wrapper">
</div>
<!--*/ Sticky Nav */-->
<nav class="sticky-nav" data-load-module="StickyNav" data-waypoint-offset=""></nav>
<!--*/ Corporate Section */-->
<section class="default-content-section">
<div class="wrapper default-content-section__container" data-analytics-container="{'blade': 'intro'}" data-exclude-section="true" data-waypoint="intro" data-waypoint-label="Introduction" id="intro">
<div>
<div class="default-content-section_heading-wrapper module-separator default-content-section_heading-wrapper--no-padding">
<header class="default-content-section_heading--left">
<h2 class="default-content-section_header hide-large" data-focus-element="true"> Introduction </h2>
</header>
</div>
</div>
<div class="text-block">
<div class="text-block__container module-separator" data-analytics-container="{'blade': 'text-block'}" data-load-module="TextBlock" data-qa-id="text-block">
<h3 class="text-block__heading"> Contact Us </h3>
<div class="rte">
<p>This Privacy Statement explains the privacy practices of Mercedes-Benz USA, LLC, its affiliates, and subsidiaries (collectively “MBUSA”) related to your access and use of MBUSA’s family of websites, widgets, and applications, collectively referred to in this Privacy Statement as the “MBUSA Platform.” In this Privacy Statement, “we,” “us,” and “our,” refer collectively to MBUSA.<br/> This Privacy Statement does not address our connected vehicle services privacy practices. Our connected vehicle services privacy practices are addressed in our <a href="/en/legal-notices/connected-vehicle">Connected Vehicle Services</a> section. Specific or additional privacy information may apply to our mobile device applications, and such information can be found in our Mobile Applications section or within the information section of the applications.</p>
<p>The MBUSA Platform is targeted to individuals in the United States and Puerto Rico. If you access the MBUSA Platform from other regions, be aware that the privacy practices of MBUSA may differ from those of your home country. By interacting with the MBUSA Platform, you are accepting the terms of this Privacy Statement. If you do not accept the terms of this Privacy Statement, do not use the MBUSA Platform.</p>
<p><b>Information You Provide to Us</b></p>
<p>Some features of the MBUSA Platform ask you to provide us with specific categories of information in order to enjoy complete functionality. If you do not provide us with the categories of information requested, your ability to fully interact with the MBUSA Platform may be limited. The features requiring you to provide information to MBUSA are described in detail below:</p>
<p><b>Inquiries</b><br/> </p>
<p>In order to submit inquiries through the MBUSA Platform, you must provide certain information. The “Contact a Dealership,” “Schedule a Test Drive,” and “Request a Quote,” forms require you to provide your name and email address. This information is required so that you can be contacted about your request. Some MBUSA Platform forms also require you to provide us with your geographic region or zip code so that we can direct your request appropriately.</p>
<p>The “Apply for <b>Financing</b>” form requires you to provide your name, address, date of birth, phone number, email address, social security number, and employment information. This information is required in order to determine your creditworthiness and to notify you of the results of your credit application.</p>
<p> </p>
<p><b>Sweepstakes, Promotions, Contests &amp; Surveys</b></p>
<p>In order to participate in sweepstakes, promotions, or contests on the MBUSA Platform, you are required to provide personal information such as your name, street address, email address, and date of birth. We require this information in order to administer the sweepstakes, promotions, and contests, to ensure participants meet applicable eligibility requirements, and to contact winners.</p>
<p>You may be asked to participate in surveys about your experience with the MBUSA Platform. When participating in surveys, any information you provide in the comments field will be shared with us, so please do not include any sensitive personal information or other information you do not wish to share.</p>
<p>Placing an Order</p>
<p> </p>
<p>When you place an order or reserve a vehicle on the MBUSA Platform, you are required to provide information necessary to fulfill that order or secure your deposit, including your name, address, phone number, and payment information. We use a third-party service to process orders, deposits, and payments. For more information, please review the “<a href="/en/legal-notices/privacy-statement#information-sharing">Information Sharing</a>” section of this Privacy Statement.</p>
<p> </p>
<p><b>Account Registration</b></p>
<p>When you register for an account with our Sites or our Applications, you must provide your name and email address. You also have the option to allow MBUSA to contact you with information about products or services that may be of interest to you. Once your account is established, you have the option to provide us with additional information such as your address and phone number so that we can pre-populate forms on the MBUSA Platform when you are logged in. You will also have the ability to save vehicle configurations and inventory favorites in your account. We store that information for as long as your account is active.</p>
<p>You may modify your accounts at any time by visiting the “Profile” settings and making changes to individual fields. You may delete your account at any time by using the “Delete My Account” link in your profile settings. Or you can <a href="/en/legal-notices/privacy-statement#contact-us">contact us</a> to modify or delete your account.</p>
<p> </p>
<p><b>Applications</b></p>
<p>When you use our Applications, you may grant certain permissions for MBUSA to obtain information from your smart device such as your location and access to your device’s camera or photos. Please consult your device manufacturer for information on how to view or modify these permissions, but note that doing so may limit the functionality of Application features.</p>
<p>In order to enjoy certain features of our Applications, you will need to provide us with the VIN from your Mercedes vehicle. This will allow us to provide you with applicable manuals, videos, connect you with a Product Concierge, and remind you of scheduled service and maintenance. On applicable models, providing your VIN will also allow you to remotely lock or unlock your vehicle, start your vehicle, play sound from your device through your vehicle, and access your vehicle’s location, mileage, and fuel information.</p>
<p>You may also link your Mercedes-Benz Financial Services account with your Mercedes me account using your social security number. MBUSA does not store your social security number when you use this function.</p>
<p>Additional information about the information you provide to us through individual Applications is available within each’s Application’s information section and <a href="/en/legal-notices/mobile-applications">here</a>.</p>
<p> </p>
<p><b>Communication Preferences</b></p>
<p>To manage your communications preferences with Mercedes-Benz USA — or to opt out of communications entirely — here’s what you’ll need to do:</p>
<p>Visit <a href="https://www.mbusa.com/en/home">https://www.mbusa.com/en/home</a> and navigate to the very bottom of the page.<br/> Enter your email address in the “Stay in Touch” section.<br/> Check your inbox for a message from Mercedes-Benz USA (it may take several minutes to arrive).<br/> Follow the instructions in our email to visit our Email Preferences page.<br/>  </p>
<p>From there, you can select exactly what you’d like to hear about, or unsubscribe from all communications.</p>
<p>To contact us with a question, call 1-800-FOR-MERCEDES (1-800-367-6372) or mail your inquiry to:</p>
<p>Mercedes-Benz USA<br/> 1 Mercedes-Benz Dr.<br/> Sandy Springs, GA, 30328</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</section>
<section class="default-content-section">
<div class="wrapper default-content-section__container" data-analytics-container="{'blade': 'information-you-provide'}" data-exclude-section="false" data-waypoint="information-you-provide" data-waypoint-label="Information You Provide to Us" id="information-you-provide">
<div>
<div class="default-content-section_heading-wrapper module-separator">
<header class="default-content-section_heading--left">
<h2 class="default-content-section_header" data-focus-element="true"> Information You Provide to Us </h2>
</header>
</div>
</div>
<div class="text-block">
<div class="text-block__container module-separator" data-analytics-container="{'blade': 'text-block'}" data-load-module="TextBlock" data-qa-id="text-block">
<div class="rte">
<p>Some features of the MBUSA Platform ask you to provide us with specific categories of information in order to enjoy complete functionality. If you do not provide us with the categories of information requested, your ability to fully interact with the MBUSA Platform may be limited. The features requiring you to provide information to MBUSA are described in detail below:</p>
<p><b>Inquiries</b></p>
<p>In order to submit inquiries through the MBUSA Platform, you must provide certain information. The “Contact a Dealership,” “Schedule a Test Drive,” and “Request a Quote,” forms require you to provide your name and email address. This information is required so that you can be contacted about your request. Some MBUSA Platform forms also require you to provide us with your geographic region or zip code so that we can direct your request appropriately.</p>
<p>The “Apply for Financing” form requires you to provide your name, address, date of birth, phone number, email address, social security number, and employment information. This information is required in order to determine your creditworthiness and to notify you of the results of your credit application.</p>
<p><b>Sweepstakes, Promotions, Contests &amp; Surveys</b></p>
<p>In order to participate in sweepstakes, promotions, or contests on the MBUSA Platform, you are required to provide personal information such as your name, street address, email address, and date of birth. We require this information in order to administer the sweepstakes, promotions, and contests, to ensure participants meet applicable eligibility requirements, and to contact winners.</p>
<p>You may be asked to participate in surveys about your experience with the MBUSA Platform. When participating in surveys, any information you provide in the comments field will be shared with us, so please do not include any sensitive personal information or other information you do not wish to share.</p>
<p><b>Placing an Order</b></p>
<p>When you place an order or reserve a vehicle on the MBUSA Platform, you are required to provide information necessary to fulfill that order or secure your deposit, including your name, address, phone number, and payment information. We use a third-party service to process orders, deposits, and payments. For more information, please review the <a href="#information-sharing">“Information Sharing”</a> section of this Privacy Statement.</p>
<p><b>Account Registration</b></p>
<p>When you register for an account with our Sites or our Applications, you must provide your name and email address. You also have the option to allow MBUSA to contact you with information about products or services that may be of interest to you. Once your account is established, you have the option to provide us with additional information such as your address and phone number so that we can pre-populate forms on the MBUSA Platform when you are logged in. You will also have the ability to save vehicle configurations and inventory favorites in your account. We store that information for as long as your account is active.</p>
<p>You may modify your accounts at any time by visiting the “Profile” settings and making changes to individual fields. You may delete your account at any time by using the “Delete My Account” link in your profile settings. Or you can <a href="#contact-us">contact us</a> to modify or delete your account.</p>
<p><b>Applications</b></p>
<p>When you use our Applications, you may grant certain permissions for MBUSA to obtain information from your smart device such as your location and access to your device’s camera or photos. Please consult your device manufacturer for information on how to view or modify these permissions, but note that doing so may limit the functionality of Application features.</p>
<p>In order to enjoy certain features of our Applications, you will need to provide us with the VIN from your Mercedes vehicle. This will allow us to provide you with applicable manuals, videos, connect you with a Product Concierge, and remind you of scheduled service and maintenance. On applicable models, providing your VIN will also allow you to remotely lock or unlock your vehicle, start your vehicle, play sound from your device through your vehicle, and access your vehicle’s location, mileage, and fuel information.</p>
<p>You may also link your Mercedes-Benz Financial Services account with your Mercedes me account using your social security number. MBUSA does not store your social security number when you use this function.</p>
<p>Additional information about the information you provide to us through individual Applications is available within each’s Application’s information section and <a href="/en/legal-notices/mobile-applications">here</a>.</p>
<p><b>Communication Preferences</b><br/> </p>
<p>To manage your communications preferences with Mercedes-Benz USA — or to opt out of communications entirely — here’s what you’ll need to do:</p>
<ol>
<li>Visit <a href="https://www.mbusa.com/en/home" target="_self">https://www.mbusa.com/en/home</a> and navigate to the very bottom of the page.</li>
<li>Enter your email address in the “Stay in Touch” section.</li>
<li>Check your inbox for a message from Mercedes-Benz USA (it may take several minutes to arrive).</li>
<li>Follow the instructions in our email to visit our Email Preferences page.</li>
</ol>
<p>From there, you can select exactly what you’d like to hear about, or unsubscribe from all communications.</p>
<p>To contact us with a question, call 1-800-FOR-MERCEDES (1-800-367-6372) or mail your inquiry to:</p>
<p>Mercedes-Benz USA</p>
<p>1 Mercedes-Benz Dr.</p>
<p>Sandy Springs, GA, 30328<br/> </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</section>
<section class="default-content-section">
<div class="wrapper default-content-section__container" data-analytics-container="{'blade': 'information-we-collect'}" data-exclude-section="false" data-waypoint="information-we-collect" data-waypoint-label="Information We Collect Automatically" id="information-we-collect">
<div>
<div class="default-content-section_heading-wrapper module-separator">
<header class="default-content-section_heading--left">
<h2 class="default-content-section_header" data-focus-element="true"> Information We Collect Automatically </h2>
</header>
</div>
</div>
<div class="text-block">
<div class="text-block__container module-separator" data-analytics-container="{'blade': 'text-block'}" data-load-module="TextBlock" data-qa-id="text-block">
<div class="rte">
<p><b>Tracking Technologies</b></p>
<p>We use cookies, pixel tags, and other tracking technologies to personalize your experience, analyze user trends, and improve the MBUSA Platform. These tracking technologies allow us to collect information such as your device type, browser type, time spent on our websites, pages visited, geographic location, and other data. These technologies also allow us to collect information about your online activities over time and across different websites or online services to tailor our products, services, and advertising to you.<br/> You can alter the configuration of your browser to refuse to accept cookies, but it is possible that doing so may cause limited functionality of the MBUSA Platform. For example, we may not be able to recognize your computer or device, and you may need to log in every time you visit.</p>
<p>The MBUSA Platform does not respond to “Do Not Track” signals at this time.</p>
<p><b>Applications</b></p>
<p>Please review the privacy statement of your device manufacturer and the privacy statement applicable to each application for information about the data automatically collected when you use our applications.</p>
<p><b>Information Collected From Third Parties</b></p>
<p>We obtain information about the traffic and usage of the MBUSA Platform from third-party service providers, including Google, Kenshoo, and Shift Digital. These third parties also use cookies and other tracking technologies to capture information about your interactions with the MBUSA Platform in addition to information about sites you have visited. These providers may place and access cookies, pixel tags, or similar technologies on your device to serve you ads or other content personalized to your interests, which they infer from your browsing on the MBUSA Platform and other sites you have visited. MBUSA does not have control over the information that is collected, used, and shared by these third parties. We encourage you to review the privacy statements of these third parties to understand their privacy practices.</p>
<p>MBUSA does not control third parties' collection or use of your information to serve interest-based advertising. However these third parties may provide you with ways to choose not to have your information collected or used in this way. You can opt out of receiving targeted ads from members of the Network Advertising Initiative ("NAI") on the NAI's <a href="http://www.networkadvertising.org/managing/opt_out.asp" style="background-color: rgb(255,255,255);">website</a>.<br/> </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</section>
<section class="default-content-section">
<div class="wrapper default-content-section__container" data-analytics-container="{'blade': 'information-sharing'}" data-exclude-section="false" data-waypoint="information-sharing" data-waypoint-label="Information Sharing" id="information-sharing">
<div>
<div class="default-content-section_heading-wrapper module-separator">
<header class="default-content-section_heading--left">
<h2 class="default-content-section_header" data-focus-element="true"> Information Sharing </h2>
</header>
</div>
</div>
<div class="text-block">
<div class="text-block__container module-separator" data-analytics-container="{'blade': 'text-block'}" data-load-module="TextBlock" data-qa-id="text-block">
<div class="rte">
<p><b>Inquiries</b></p>
<p>When you complete the “Contact a Dealership,” “Schedule a Test Drive,” or “Request a Quote,” forms, we share the information you provide with authorized dealerships so they can contact you about your request and provide you with information about services and products that may meet your needs. When you complete the “Apply for <b>Financing</b>” form, your information is shared with Mercedes-Benz Financial Services so that it can review your credit application. Information about Mercedes-Benz Financial Services’ privacy practices is available <u><a href="https://mbfs.com/creditapp/termsAndConditions" target="_blank">here</a></u>.<br/> </p>
<p><b>Sweepstakes, Promotions, Contests &amp; Surveys</b><br/> </p>
<p>We use third party service providers to manage MBUSA Platform-based sweepstakes, promotions, and contests, and to conduct surveys about your experience using the MBUSA Platform or our other products and services. When you enter sweepstakes, promotions, and contests or complete surveys on the MBUSA Platform, your information is shared with our service providers, which may include our authorized dealerships and our affiliates and their subcontractors.<br/> </p>
<p><b>Placing an Order</b></p>
<p>We use third party service providers to manage our Lifestyle Collection website and to manage deposit payments when you reserve a vehicle. Information you provide when making online purchases is shared with our third party service providers so that your payment can be processed and your order can be fulfilled.<br/> </p>
<p><b>Account Registration</b></p>
<p>When you register an account on the MBUSA Platform, MBUSA does not maintain your password. That information is stored on Mercedes-Benz AG’s customer identity and access management system. Some of our connected vehicle application features are managed by third party service providers. If you register through the MBUSA Platform, your information will be provided to the Mercedes-Benz Group and third parties with whom you choose to link your account information to subscribe to or use their services.<br/> </p>
<p><b>Authentication Services</b></p>
<p>We may share your ID and other personal information with our ID verification service providers, who may use facial recognition software to verify your identity.<br/> </p>
<p><b>Third Party Links</b><br/> </p>
<p>The MBUSA Platform contains links to other websites such as social media platforms, other Mercedes-Benz websites, and event and partner websites. These websites are not covered by MBUSA’s Privacy Statement. Please review the Privacy Statements of these websites in order to understand the privacy practices of these third parties.<br/> </p>
<p><b>Applications</b></p>
<p>Please review the privacy statement of your device manufacturer and the privacy statement applicable to each application for information about the data shared from our applications.<br/> </p>
<p><b>Vehicle Services Providers</b></p>
<p>We offer various vehicle-related services through the MBUSA Platform and your information may be shared with third party service providers in order to provide you with a specific service.<br/> </p>
<p><b>Other</b><br/> </p>
<p>Aside from the instances described above, we will only share your personal information: to comply with the law; to respond to claims; to comply with legal process served on MBUSA or our parent company Mercedes-Benz AG (e.g., a lawful subpoena, warrant, or court order); to enforce or apply our policies or agreements; (including to bill and collect payments); to protect and defend our rights or property or that of our dealers, customers, employees, visitors, or the public; in connection with a business transfer, sale, liquidation, or merger; and if we reasonably believe that an emergency involving immediate danger of death or serious physical injury to any person requires disclosure; with your consent.<br/> </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</section>
